[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m768[0m[39m:        PreMin = PostMin = [0m[32m""[0m[39m;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m769[0m[39m:        break;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m23[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m24[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[95m------------------------------------------------------------------------------[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [95m---[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m25[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m26[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m27[0m[39m:#include [0m[32m"lcms2_internal.h"[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m28[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m29[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m PostScript ColorRenderingDictionary and ColorSpaceArray[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m30[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m31[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m32[0m[39m:#define MAXPSCOLS   [0m[1;36m60[0m[39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Columns on tables[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m33[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m34[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[39m*[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m35[0m[39m:    Implementation[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m36[0m[39m:    --------------[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m37[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m38[0m[39m:  PostScript does use XYZ as its internal PCS. But since PostScript[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m39[0m[39m:  interpolation tables are limited to [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m bits, I use Lab as a way to[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m40[0m[39m:  improve the accuracy, favoring perceptual results. So, for the creation[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m41[0m[39m:  of each CRD, CSA the profiles are converted to Lab via a device[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m42[0m[39m:  link between  profile -> Lab or Lab -> profile. The PS code necessary to[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m43[0m[39m:  convert Lab <-> XYZ is also included.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m44[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m45[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m46[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m47[0m[39m:  Color Space Arrays [0m[1;39m([0m[39mCSA[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m48[0m[39m:  [0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m==================================================================================[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m49[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m50[0m[39m:  In order to obtain precision, code chooses between three ways to implement[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m51[0m[39m:  the device -> XYZ transform. These cases identifies monochrome profiles [0m[1;39m([0m[39moften[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m52[0m[39m:  implemented as a set of curves[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, matrix-shaper and Pipeline-based.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m53[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m54[0m[39m:  Monochrome[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m55[0m[39m:  -----------[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m56[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m57[0m[39m:  This is implemented as [0m[35m/[0m[95mCIEBasedA[0m[39m CSA. The prelinearization curve is[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m58[0m[39m:  placed into [0m[35m/[0m[95mDecodeA[0m[39m section, and matrix equals to D50. Since here is[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m59[0m[39m:  no interpolation tables, I do the conversion directly to XYZ[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m60[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m61[0m[39m:  NOTE: CLUT-based monochrome profiles are NOT supported. So, [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcmsFLAGS_MATRIXIN[0m[1;33mPUT[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m62[0m[39m:  flag is forced on such profiles.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m63[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m64[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m[[0m[39m [0m[35m/[0m[95mCIEBasedA[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m65[0m[39m:      <<[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m66[0m[39m:            [0m[35m/[0m[95mDecodeA[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m transfer function [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m bind[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m67[0m[39m:            [0m[35m/[0m[95mMatrixA[0m[39m [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mD50[0m[1;39m][0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m68[0m[39m:            [0m[35m/[0m[95mRangeLMN[0m[39m [0m[1;39m[[0m[39m [0m[1;36m0.0[0m[39m cmsD50X [0m[1;36m0.0[0m[39m cmsD50Y [0m[1;36m0.0[0m[39m cmsD50Z [0m[1;39m][0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m69[0m[39m:            [0m[35m/[0m[95mWhitePoint[0m[39m [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mD50[0m[1;39m][0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m70[0m[39m:            [0m[35m/[0m[95mBlackPoint[0m[39m [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mBP[0m[1;39m][0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m71[0m[39m:            [0m[35m/[0m[95mRenderingIntent[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mintent[0m[1;39m)[0m                                            [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis of the Issue[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter examining the evaluation report and relevant code snippets, I've identified [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe root cause of the null pointer dereference vulnerability:[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe crash occurs in `EmitCIEBasedDEF` [0m[1;39m([0m[39msrc/cmsps2.[0m[1;92mc:795[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m where `[0m[1;35mcmsStageType[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis called on a potentially NULL pointer. The sequence is:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Line [0m[1;36m761[0m[39m: `mpe = Pipeline->Elements` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mget first stage[0m[1;39m)[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Line [0m[1;36m786[0m[39m: Check if first stage is CurveSet type[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Line [0m[1;36m792[0m[39m: If yes, advance to next stage: `mpe = mpe->Next`[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m795[0m[39m: Call `[0m[1;35mcmsStageType[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` WITHOUT null check** â† CRASH HERE[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe pipeline optimization process [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`_cmsOptimizePipeline` in src/cmsopt.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m can [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremove or consolidate stages, potentially leaving only a CurveSet stage with no [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfollowing CLUT stage. When this happens, `mpe->Next` returns NULL, and the [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msubsequent `[0m[1;35mcmsStageType[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` dereferences NULL+[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39moffset to Type field[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, causing [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe crash at address [0m[1;36m0x000000000008[0m[39m.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Critical Logic to Preserve[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The PostScript CSA generation logic for [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m4[0m[39m channel profiles[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. The optional CurveSet stage handling [0m[1;39m([0m[39mDecodeDEF emission[0m[1;39m)[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. The optional CLUT stage handling [0m[1;39m([0m[39mTable emission[0m[1;39m)[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. The Lab2XYZ conversion and metadata emission[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. The existing optimization pipeline must continue to work[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Comprehensive Fix Strategy[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Fix: Add Null Pointer Check in EmitCIEBasedDEF[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location:** `src/cmsps2.c`, function `EmitCIEBasedDEF` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m753[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m810[0m[1;39m)[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m:** Add null pointer validation after line [0m[1;36m792[0m[39m, before line [0m[1;36m795[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter the line `mpe = mpe->Next;` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m792[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, add a null check before calling [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mcmsStageType[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` at line [0m[1;36m795[0m[39m. The fix should:[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Check if `mpe` is NULL after advancing to the next stage[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Only proceed with CLUT emission if `mpe` is non-NULL[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Maintain the existing behavior when stages are present[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Implementation approach:**[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Insert a null check between lines [0m[1;36m793[0m[39m and [0m[1;36m795[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Wrap the CLUT processing block [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m795[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m800[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in a condition that checks `mpe !=[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNULL`[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This preserves the optional nature of both CurveSet and CLUT stages[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Pseudo-logic:**[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mcmsStageType[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == cmsSigCurveSetElemType[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Emit DecodeDEF[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    mpe = mpe->Next;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m ADD NULL CHECK HERE[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe != NULL && [0m[1;35mcmsStageType[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == cmsSigCLutElemType[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Emit Table[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This is Optimal[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Minimal Change:** Only adds a null check where needed, preserving all existing[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Defensive Programming:** Follows the principle of validating pointers before [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdereferencing[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Consistent with Design:** The code already treats both CurveSet and CLUT as [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moptional [0m[1;39m([0m[39musing `if` statements, not `if-else`[0m[1;39m)[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Matches Documentation:** The PostScript CSA format documentation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m105[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m117[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m shows that [0m[35m/[0m[95mDecodeDEF[0m[39m is optional, and [0m[35m/[0m[95mTable[0m[39m should also be optional[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **No Breaking Changes:** Existing test cases and functionality are preserved[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **Handles Edge Cases:** Properly handles pipelines with only CurveSet, only [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCLUT, both, or neither[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Preserves Existing Logic[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The function still processes CurveSet stages when present [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m786[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m793[0m[1;39m)[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The function still processes CLUT stages when present [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m795[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m800[0m[1;39m)[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Lab2XYZ conversion and metadata emission continue unchanged [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m802[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m809[0m[1;39m)[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Return value remains [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39msuccess[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m as before[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The PostScript output format remains valid even without a CLUT section[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Addresses Evaluation Report Issues[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Fixes the crash:** Prevents `cmsStageType` from being called on NULL pointer[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Handles optimization side effects:** Accounts for pipelines where optimization[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremoved CLUT stages[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Maintains API compatibility:** No changes to function signatures or calling [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Preserves [0m[33mSCARINESS[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m10[0m[39m protection:** Eliminates the null-deref vulnerability[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effect [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m:** PostScript output may not include [0m[35m/[0m[95mTable[0m[39m section[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Mitigation:** This is correct behavior - [0m[35m/[0m[95mTable[0m[39m is optional in CIEBasedDEF [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mformat[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Validation:** The PostScript specification allows CSA without lookup tables[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effect [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m:** Profiles relying on CLUT may produce different output[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Mitigation:** The optimization pipeline already determines when CLUT is needed[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Validation:** If optimization removes CLUT, it's because the transform can be [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrepresented without it[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effect [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m:** Empty pipelines [0m[1;39m([0m[39mboth stages NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Mitigation:** Already handled - function still emits valid PostScript with [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mLab2XYZ conversion[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Validation:** EmitLab2XYZ [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m802[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m provides fallback conversion[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar Solutions in Codebase[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix follows the pattern used in `GenerateCSA` [0m[1;39m([0m[39msrc/cmsps2.[0m[1;92mc:1071[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1075[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m which [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muses `cmsPipelineCheckAndRetreiveStages` to validate pipeline structure before [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maccessing stages. While we don't need the full validation function here, the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprinciple of checking before dereferencing is the same pattern used throughout the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcodebase.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAdditionally, other emit functions like `EmitCIEBasedA` and `EmitCIEBasedABC` [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreceive pre-validated parameters, avoiding direct pipeline manipulation. This fix [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbrings `EmitCIEBasedDEF` closer to that safer pattern by adding validation.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Implementation Steps from Initial Codebase[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Locate `src/cmsps2.c` line [0m[1;36m795[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Modify the condition from:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mcmsStageType[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == cmsSigCLutElemType[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   to:[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe != NULL && [0m[1;35mcmsStageType[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmpe[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == cmsSigCLutElemType[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Verify the fix compiles without warnings[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Test with the fuzzer input to confirm crash is resolved[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Run existing test suite to ensure no regressions[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is a surgical fix that addresses the exact vulnerability without modifying [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzing logic, test code, utility functions, or external dependencies. The fix is [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapplied only to the source code that contains the bug, maintaining full backward [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompatibility.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
